        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780451490803" href="/book/show/36577586-the-kiss-quotient">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2433591253" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17683613104683126640">well, if this wasnt just the most wholesome story i have read in a while. my goodness. this was so pure. <br/><br/>i think romance books have improved so much lately. its been quite wonderful to see romance stories with so much depth to them, beyond just two people in love/lust. not that the swoon-worthy parts arent great, but now i can actually say i read the books for the plot, and mean it. :P<br/><br/>what i really enjoyed about this book, specifically, was getting the opportunity to read from the perspective of</span>
  <span id="freeText17683613104683126640" style="display:none">well, if this wasnt just the most wholesome story i have read in a while. my goodness. this was so pure. <br /><br />i think romance books have improved so much lately. its been quite wonderful to see romance stories with so much depth to them, beyond just two people in love/lust. not that the swoon-worthy parts arent great, but now i can actually say i read the books for the plot, and mean it. :P<br /><br />what i really enjoyed about this book, specifically, was getting the opportunity to read from the perspective of character who has autism. having such a unique character made it very interesting to read about how differently emotions can be processed and interrupted. this story made me think about what romance means to not only me, but other people. i will admit, at times the plot was a little unrealistic. but i thought the characters were the most real thing about this story. they felt very authentic and genuine and helped the story feel more natural. <br /><br />after reading this, i can completely understand the massive attention this book has gotten over the past few months. its the perfect story for those looking for a lovely feel-good book to end their summer!<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>4 stars</i></b></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=berkley">berkley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2356309640" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11985415819386727580">The Kiss Quotient by Helen Hoang is a 2018 Berkley publication. <br/><br/>A real charmer!<br/><br/>Stella, an Econometrician, has intimacy issues, perhaps a symptom of her Asperger’s. With her mother growing impatient for grandchildren, and after absorbing an ugly comment, which took aim at Stella’s lack of sexual experience, she decides to hire a male escort to ‘teach’ her everything she needs to know about dating and sex. <br/><br/>Michael Phan has never had a client like Stella. She touches a part of him, he keeps barrica</span>
  <span id="freeText11985415819386727580" style="display:none">The Kiss Quotient by Helen Hoang is a 2018 Berkley publication. <br /><br />A real charmer!<br /><br />Stella, an Econometrician, has intimacy issues, perhaps a symptom of her Asperger’s. With her mother growing impatient for grandchildren, and after absorbing an ugly comment, which took aim at Stella’s lack of sexual experience, she decides to hire a male escort to ‘teach’ her everything she needs to know about dating and sex. <br /><br />Michael Phan has never had a client like Stella. She touches a part of him, he keeps barricaded, especially with clients. Her effect on him is so powerful, he agrees to give her lessons on sex and dating, against his better judgment, and breaking every single personal rule of his profession.<br /><br />However, their business arrangement soon develops into something neither of them could have anticipated. Before long, Stella begins to figure in a new type of equation- love!<br /><br />Okay, I’ve seen the huge marketing push for the book, and I’ve had many friends on social media and book sites fawning it. From experience I know when a book gets this level of hype it is very important to approach it with a modicum of caution. Even though I was chomping at the bit to start this one, pushing everything else to the wayside if need be, I cooled my engines and let some of the furor die down before I finally allowed myself to read it. <br /><br />So, did it live up to all that publicity?<br /><br />I adored this story. It’s unique, featuring a female character who struggles to find her niche in a world that embraces conformity and uniformity. I don’t have Asperger’s syndrome, but I am an extreme introvert, so I could relate to some of the struggles Stella fought to overcome. I immediately warmed to her character and hoped she would find the confidence she had buried inside of her all along.<br /><br />While I didn’t know how to feel about Michael’s unorthodox occupation, I did LOVE this guy’s gentle patience. It was fun watching Stella crawl under his skin, seeing how he understood her, quirks and all, and how they managed to create a relationship with each other, as Michael slowly draws Stella out. Michael turned out to be a terrific hero, and I might have developed a secret and deliciously sinful crush on him. <br /><br />That said, the book was still a wee bit over-hyped. While I understand why some felt this one was special and deserved a lot of attention, the format, at its core, is not much different from any other contemporary romance. The writing or prose didn't set it apart from any other books out there, although it is obvious the author knew her subject matter intimately. <br /><br />What does set it apart is the diversity, and the boldness of placing a character with Asperger’s as a lead in a romantic comedy. The delicate balance of approaching the syndrome with respect and the gravity it deserves, while adding in humor and poignancy, is very well done. From that perspective the story is very original, unique, and refreshing! <br /><br />Everything you love about romance is here: It's hot and steamy, funny, charming, emotional, and inspiring, with a lovely feel good ending. <br /><br />However, this one gives voice to those rarely featured in these types of stories. I love that about this book!! I for one, applaud this new angle and approach to contemporary romance, and hope to see more books step away from the standard 'Plain Jane' tropes and branch out into new, mostly unexplored territory, in the romance genre. Books like this one could help the genre shake off a few of its hardwired stigmas and reach a much broader audience. <br /><br /> 4.5 stars<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11985415819386727580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13709877518389278570" style="display:none">This book was so easy to love; I can see why it's getting all the attention it so richly deserves. <i>The Kiss Quotient</i> is the perfect example of own voices that we desperately crave more of. <div id="review_2430867841" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2430867841" />
    <a title="Meredith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30978160-meredith"><img alt="Meredith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423329725p2/30978160.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2430867841?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Meredith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Meredith" href="/user/show/30978160-meredith">Meredith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2430867841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17241887365930714187"><b>
  <i>3.5 stars <br/><br/>To sum up my reading experience of The Kiss Quotient, I would have to say it’s like, not love.<br/><br/>I really wanted to love The Kiss Quotient. While I enjoyed it, I didn’t love it. I think the hype ruined it for me, as I had mighty high expectations going into this. </i>
</b><br/><br/>25-year-old econometrician Stella has autism; she’s high functioning but has trouble with social skills and intimacy, amongst other issues. Her mother wants grandbabies and pressures her to date. But Stella does not enjoy dat</span>
  <span id="freeText17241887365930714187" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>3.5 stars <br /><br />To sum up my reading experience of The Kiss Quotient, I would have to say it’s like, not love.<br /><br />I really wanted to love The Kiss Quotient. While I enjoyed it, I didn’t love it. I think the hype ruined it for me, as I had mighty high expectations going into this. </i>
</b><br /><br />25-year-old econometrician Stella has autism; she’s high functioning but has trouble with social skills and intimacy, amongst other issues. Her mother wants grandbabies and pressures her to date. But Stella does not enjoy dating, nor does she like sex. When someone suggests to Stella that she practice honing her sexual skills, she takes their advice and hires male escort Michael, to teach her what she does not know. Michael happens to have a conscious and quickly realizes that Stella is different than the other woman that hire him. Genuinely wanting to help Stella, he goes against his rule of spending only one night with a client and allows Stella to book him for multiple sessions. The two fall in love, but must fight through their insecurities to stay together.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“She had a disorder, but it didn’t define her. She was Stella. She was a unique person.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Stella’s character is what makes <i>The Kiss Quotient</i> stand out from other romances. It’s clear Hoang did her research and seamlessly incorporates Stella’s insecurities stemming from her autism. Autistic women don’t usually show up in romances, and Hoang takes a risk with Stella’s character. I also really liked Michael’s character; Hoang truly creates Stella’s perfect match with Michael.<br /><br />This is fast-paced, addictive, easy read. The premise is a little out there, but it makes sense especially after reading Hoang’s Author’s note. I just wish it hadn’t been so predictable. I saw how everything could play out very early on the book but <b>I was hoping that Stella and Michael’s romance would take a different path; one that is as unique as their characters. </b> Outside of Stella having autism, I feel like I have read books like this before. I was hoping for something a little more outside of the box, but it was overly predictable. <b>Overall, I found this to be a fun, fluffy, and unfortunately, formulaic read.</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17241887365930714187" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2415013184" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2415013184" />
    <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog"><img alt="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465210954p2/41356020.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2415013184?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog">Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=third-pov">third-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=fake-relationship">fake-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=escort">escort</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2415013184" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12543631835889105043"><b>10 perfect stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528298528i/25672299._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a href='http://www.ofpensandpages.com/2018/06/the-kiss-quotient-helen-hoang.html/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review & Excerpt at Of Pens and Pages.</a><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434495937i/15229948.jpg' width='25' height='25”' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  <i>All the things that make you different make you perfect.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I am in love. <i>The Kiss Quotient</i> is a beautiful and realistic debut novel that breaks stereotypes, embraces uniqueness, and makes one think about their self-worth. It’s the kind of book that will make you smile, swoon, tear up, and think. I was on cloud nine when I finished it. It’s been a few days since I finished reading this book, and I’m still on a high! I haven’t read anythi</span>
  <span id="freeText12543631835889105043" style="display:none"><b>10 perfect stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528298528i/25672299._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.ofpensandpages.com/2018/06/the-kiss-quotient-helen-hoang.html/" rel="nofollow noopener">Review &amp; Excerpt at Of Pens and Pages.</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434495937i/15229948.jpg" width="25" height="25”" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <i>All the things that make you different make you perfect.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I am in love. <i>The Kiss Quotient</i> is a beautiful and realistic debut novel that breaks stereotypes, embraces uniqueness, and makes one think about their self-worth. It’s the kind of book that will make you smile, swoon, tear up, and think. I was on cloud nine when I finished it. It’s been a few days since I finished reading this book, and I’m still on a high! I haven’t read anything since. It took me so long to articulate my thoughts, and I still don’t think I gave this book justice, but let me try.<br><br>Stella Lane may be a well-paid and successful econometrician, but for her mother, nothing would be better than for Stella to finally give her parents some grand-babies. Babies mean intimacy and sex, two things Stella isn’t particularly well-versed. If she’s going to take her mother’s request seriously, she’s going to need to learn the ins and outs of sex. No pun intended.<br><br>Who better to teach her than Michael? The beautiful man who can give Daniel Henney a run for his money definitely knows sex; he gets paid to seduce women and pleasure them. So she hires him to teach her. What Stella doesn’t consider is that maybe she’s looking at it the wrong way. Maybe it isn’t just sex she needs to learn, but relationships itself.<br><br>Michael only sticks to doing his night job on Fridays, and never with the same client more than once. Stella’s request breaks so much of his personal rules, but he can’t help but say yes. The effect he felt the short time he spent with Stella was unlike anything he’s ever felt before. But those feelings need to get out of the way because he can’t have her. Stella is smart, rich, and beautiful, and she deserves so much more. Not a man with a past he continues to escape.<br><br>As they go on with Love and Relationship 101, Stella and Michael learn so much more than what’s in their lesson plan. They learn about each other, and they both like it very much. Now, they just have to decide whether to pursue the real deal or not.<br><br>This book is heartwarming, sweet, and angstier and steamier than I expected. And I’m not mad about it at all. This book made me tear up more than once because of Stella and Michael and how perfect they are for each other. To see two people so in sync and see how much they’re helping each other is heartwarming. It isn’t one-sided. Michael needs Stella as much as she needs him. <br><br>I love Stella and Michael so much. Words aren’t enough to express my feelings about them. Stella is strong, endearing, and so precious. She’s a genuinely nice person, thoughtful and nurturing to others. As a person on the autism spectrum, she has issues with social interactions that can sometimes give the wrong impression to others; worse case scenario, it hurts or offends them. It’s not something she does on purpose, and she tries her best to be aware of her words and actions to keep it from happening again. My heart went out for her that she had to hide her condition, afraid that people might see and treat her differently.<br><br>Sweet Michael. He’s everything I want and more. This man is hard-working, loyal to the core, sweet, and oh my Lord is he hot. This man will make your heart and panties fall, you guys. Such a cinnamon roll. And the tongue on this one. I am fanning myself right now!<br><br>And I just have to say I love his family. It was such a delight to see the Vietnamese side of his family, their interaction with each other so genuine and fantastic. I’m looking forward to getting to know Khai in <i>The Bride Test</i>!<br><br>With an engaging writing, amazing chemistry, and relatable characters you’ll fall in love with, <i>The Kiss Quotient</i> is a book you need to read. A perfect summer read. A perfect read for any time of the year, really. It’s definitely one of the highlights of my year! <i>The Kiss Quotient</i> is something I will never forget and will forever cherish in my heart. You need to read this book. I promise you won’t regret meeting Stella and Michael. <br><br><b>Tropes:</b> Escort, Fake Relationship<br><b>POV:</b>Third Person, Dual POV<br><b>Standalone:</b> Yes<br><br><i>*ARC received in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><a href="http://ofpensandpages.com" rel="nofollow noopener"> Blog</a> | <a href="http://facebook.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="http://twitter.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/nissareads" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12543631835889105043" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2826521067" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13299865224657639746"><b>The Kiss Quotient was heartwarming, charming and quite steamy!</b> <br/><br/>Stella Lane was completely endearing. She is smart, driven and living with high-functioning Aspergers. She also has relationship and intimacy issues. How does one overcome those? With a master teacher of course. Enter Michael Phan. He is suave, sexually experienced and a male escort. Sound familiar? It definitely had a flipped Pretty Woman vibe and you know what - it totally worked!<br/><br/>Amidst their <i>"lessons"</i>, Stella and Michael discover </span>
  <span id="freeText13299865224657639746" style="display:none"><b>The Kiss Quotient was heartwarming, charming and quite steamy!</b> <br /><br />Stella Lane was completely endearing. She is smart, driven and living with high-functioning Aspergers. She also has relationship and intimacy issues. How does one overcome those? With a master teacher of course. Enter Michael Phan. He is suave, sexually experienced and a male escort. Sound familiar? It definitely had a flipped Pretty Woman vibe and you know what - it totally worked!<br /><br />Amidst their <i>"lessons"</i>, Stella and Michael discover there is much more to each other than meets the eye. They were just so cute together. Michael so patient, understanding and caring of Stella's need. In turn, Stella truly seeing him for who he is - encouraging him and accepting him. Is that a bit idealistic? Yes, it is but this is a romance novel. Isn't that part of its appeal. I easily got lost in their romance and found myself rooting for them to have their happily ever after. 🥰<br /><br /><b>Helen Hoang has firmly rooted herself as a must read author for me.</b> We are 2 for 2 with her novels and I am beyond excited as I anticipate book #3 with one of my FAVORITE &amp; swoon-worthy side characters! Write quickly Ms. Hoang - your readers are anxiously awaiting more steamy, romantic goodness!!!!</span>

<div id="review_2427823518" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2427823518?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781683319139" href="/book/show/40500960-the-kiss-quotient">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2427823518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18381376942411459213"><b>**4.5-steamy stars rounded up**</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561384059ra/27718928.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book filled my heart and just when I thought it couldn't get any better, it did! <br/><br/>My cup runneth over. Thank you, Michael Phan. I love you.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576078495ra/28595345.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Focus, Meg, focus!<br/><br/>Feeling pressure from her parents, Stella Lane, decides she needs help in the relationship department. <br/><br/>She's of a 'certain age' and they, especially her mom, are expecting things from her.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576078495ra/28595346.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Stella, who has Asperger's, finds direct contact and intimacy extremely difficult. <br/><br/>She is hoping with some professional </span>
  <span id="freeText18381376942411459213" style="display:none"><b>**4.5-steamy stars rounded up**</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561384059ra/27718928.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book filled my heart and just when I thought it couldn't get any better, it did! <br><br>My cup runneth over. Thank you, Michael Phan. I love you.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576078495ra/28595345.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Focus, Meg, focus!<br><br>Feeling pressure from her parents, Stella Lane, decides she needs help in the relationship department. <br><br>She's of a 'certain age' and they, especially her mom, are expecting things from her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576078495ra/28595346.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Stella, who has Asperger's, finds direct contact and intimacy extremely difficult. <br><br>She is hoping with some professional guidance, she can at least learn well enough to make it work with an appropriate match. <br><br>Therefore, she hires a male escort to teach her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1549629108ra/27033598.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As you do...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1579292780ra/28795974.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Introducing Michael Phan, who I literally fell in love with in the first 20-pages of the story. <br><br>Instalove much?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576078495ra/28595347.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The reader gets taken on a journey through Stella and Michael's sessions that will leave you thinking, maybe Stella is on to something. <br><br>Michael was so kind and had such patience with her, I dare you not to find him attractive.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576078667ra/28595350.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The scenes were steamy but still tender in an oddly compelling way. <br><br>There is a lot of dirty talk though, so if that is not your thing, you maybe want to avoid this but otherwise, give it a shot!<br><br>Obviously, towards the end, I did get frustrated a bit with the lack of communication between the characters, but I understand you need some drama.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1579293029ra/28795984.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Ultimately, I was very pleased with the conclusion!<br><br>I would definitely recommend this to other Adult Romance readers, although I feel like I am actually the last one to read it. <br><br>I am really looking forward to continuing on with the companion novels in this series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487259430ra/21992826.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_2415314764" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2415314764" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2415314764?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2415314764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4955676460207513784"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1490616663ra/22327288.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> “I don't want just a night or a week or a month with you. <br/>I want you all the time. <br/>I like you better than calculus, and math is the only thing that unites the universe.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/><i> Asperger Syndrome <br/>- a developmental disorder characterized by severely impaired social skills, repetitive behaviors, and often, a narrow set of interests, but not involving delayed development of linguistic and cognitive abilities </i> <br/>Readers often criticize that there isn’t enough representation of certain charact</span>
  <span id="freeText4955676460207513784" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1490616663ra/22327288.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> “I don't want just a night or a week or a month with you. <br>I want you all the time. <br>I like you better than calculus, and math is the only thing that unites the universe.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> Asperger Syndrome <br>- a developmental disorder characterized by severely impaired social skills, repetitive behaviors, and often, a narrow set of interests, but not involving delayed development of linguistic and cognitive abilities </i> <br>Readers often criticize that there isn’t enough representation of certain characters in books. Starting with lgbt 🏳️‍🌈 characters and continuing with several psychological disorders - one of it being Asperger. <br>I’m no professional at this issue, I only know the definition and some people who have it, but in my opinion this was a great representation of it. <br>The whole story is about Michael and Stella. <br>Stella is a successful business woman who works in econometrics. Her life seems good: she earns a great amount of money, has a great pair of parents and is beautiful and extremely smart. But there is one thing that never really works for her: Men. <br>So one day she decides to take an escort to teach her how to have great sex. And with this decision she meets Michael, an escort for every type of woman. But only on Friday. Until he meets Stella and falls deeply in love with her.<br>Whoa, this book is the perfect balance of sex, love and drama. Whoah, guys. If your prude or don’t want to read something smutty, then don’t read this book! <br>Because 🔥🔥🔥<br>This book Is hot and sweet and everything you wish for. <br>I really really liked it, but in my opinion there could’ve been a little bit more action. More drama.<br><br>Character ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “He has a mixed Vietnamese and Swedish heritage, that makes him look like the K-Drama star Daniel Henney.” </i> <br>Because I didn’t have a clue who that person above is, I googled him and found this: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528919101ra/25771716.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And whoah (that’s the second time is said that) my imagination was right, Michael is a really good looking and handsome character. <br>And with his cute smile, which makes all the hearts explode, he’s even cuter.<br>I like that the author makes him a in some way arrogant but still likable character. <br>He’s kindhearted, charming and gives so much love to everyone around him. <br>That makes him so precious 💕<br>Next to him Stella is even more lovable. She’s so smart and a little bit weird and that makes her so adorable and awesome. She’s successful, smart, honest and still she’s a sensitive and friendly person with a big but rightful heart. <br>I fell in love with her on the front page and it didn’t change throughout the book. <br>These two were the most adorable couple I’ve read in a while ♥️<br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Wow, this was so hot 🔥 <br>Phew. Phew. Phew. 💥💥💥<br>The author is great at writing sexy scenes, that’s all I can say. <br>I don’t want to spoiler you, (but it’s obvious - it’s a contemporary) but I love these two together. <br>I mean their relationship was adorable, wonderful and so beautiful. And so pure. <br>I mean, most of their problems were caused by huge misunderstandings and misinterpreted feelings and words. <br>But again, there wouldn’t be no drama without these things. <br>So, all in all, I loved the love in this story♥️ <br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Well, that was beautiful. It was simple with a nice flow and pacing. The chapters are not that long, so you literally flow through the book. <br>I finished it in just a few days and I’m so happy with it. <br>It’s not my favorite, The hating game is unchallenged, but it was still wonderful and some time later I’ll definitely reread it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528918955ra/25771697.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4955676460207513784" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DIm9WuNizNlfkKakRBcHCm/Q1sFxle8eOzWsjH/GJsJ5iqqV2Gmf+4tXPDfN2nBDJ00yHMN4JLOoVhze4ViIqw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ebbcvtVfy/2tkVL4/xAXv6GfGYRkFHtwIMjMBv+/IloMtctx7lSY33lWyGt23WD26QL9Wdb5sN2zq3xUYSGMMw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer18045255995102291587">Helen Hoang is that shy person who never talks. Until she does. And the worst things fly out of her mouth. She read her first romance novel in eighth grade and has been addicted ever since. In 2016, she was diagnosed with Autism Spectrum Disorder in line with what was previously known as Asperger’s Syndrome. Her journey inspired THE KISS QUOTIENT. She currently lives in San Diego, California with </span>
  <span id="freeText18045255995102291587" style="display:none">Helen Hoang is that shy person who never talks. Until she does. And the worst things fly out of her mouth. She read her first romance novel in eighth grade and has been addicted ever since. In 2016, she was diagnosed with Autism Spectrum Disorder in line with what was previously known as Asperger’s Syndrome. Her journey inspired THE KISS QUOTIENT. She currently lives in San Diego, California with her husband, two kids, and pet fish.</span>
